<text>I brought in 2006 TL that had died while driving, electronics and engine shutoff and coasted to a stop.  However, after brief time it started right back up and ran like nothing happened.  Took it into my local auto repair shop that has handled all repairs to this point.  However, they could not get the problem to reoccur, and also could not figure out prior problems where battery dies if don't start car for more than 24 hours, and the Vehicle Stabilization Assist (VSA) trouble light was on.

So, I picked my car up and did some research on Acura dealers and after reading reviews decided to go a little farther to Thomas Acura.  They fixed the battery draw problem (disconnected HFU), and the VSA light right away.  However, they also couldn't get the car to shutoff while driving after testing for 3 days.  They didn't want to replace a part without knowing it was going to fix the problem (which I appreciated), but after I asked them possible causes from their previous experience with TLs, I decided to have them replace a portion of the Ignition switch that is the most probable reason for an intermittent electrical shutdown.

It was also time to replace the tires, and they carried the brand I wanted and installed them for very competitive price.  The total for all this work was very reasonable, and they fixed everything that I asked them, and didn't push to fix anything else. < Review>
Bought my new 2013 RDX from Thomas Acura. I worked with JR the sales person and Zabi the sales manager. Both are friendly, funny and easy to work with.

After some internet search, i narrowed down the price range for how much i wanted to pay for this vehicle. I sent out price inquiries to a bunch of Acura dealers around town, and got a few quotes including Thomas Acura. Thomas wasn't the lowest offer, but they were able to beat it by another $100. Everything went so smooth with ZERO back-and-forth typical dealer haggle. JR and I exchanged a few emails and got everything agreed upon before i went to pick up the vehicle. When i arrived, JR greeted me with my brand new RDX. He spent a good 20 minutes going thru all the features with me, very thoroughly. Unlike many other sales I met who only cared about $$$ and sales, JR knows the product inside-out. The price was exactly what i was quoted, and he did not push to sell me anything i didn't need.

Zabi, the sales manager, took care of all my paperwork. He's efficient and funny. It took less than an hour to go thru all the documents, and his jokes made the whole process like cruising on a Hawaiian sunset boat.

Overall, the experience of buying my new RDX with Thomas Acura has been nothing but pleasant. I highly recommend JR Davidson and Razi. Do your homework, get prepared and work with Thomas Acura. Not only will you get your loved new car, but with ease and smile.<//Review>

< text>
Can't go wrong with some Ben's. Everything was quick and delicious as usual. Our order usually consists of a family size fries (they don't salt them, you do), a Western Burger (onion rings, cheese, BBQ sauce, bacon), a Hawaiian Burger (pineapple, cheese, teriyaki sauce) and a couple grilled cheese sandwiches. They make their shakes with hand scooped ice cream, and have bananas and malt if you want to add them. We typically have a Rocky Road and a couple Cookies and Cream. I ventured out and had a Banana & Chocolate Malt ü§§... See you soon Ben's Burgers...< /text>

< review>
This place is not fast food, do not put it in that category.  My wife and I love this place and miss it dearly.   We live elsewhere now but still haven't found a burger joint that is quite like this one.  Ben has the best teriyaki burger on the planet.   The milkshakes and fries here are great compliments to the burgers.   I think Foster freezer has the best fries.  Not many of them around anymore.   Ben's fries aren't greasy and mirror Foster's the best.  Look no further you have found the perfect place.<//review>

A few months into my lease, several units were broken into, over $12k stolen from my unit, items that my deceased parents had given me and other valuables that I can never get back. One of the units near mine, the poor guy lost his whole apartment (he was away traveling). Horrific! The Bay Area has such high crime but why are the storage rents here so low? It's because the security is basically nonexistent and they don't care about break-ins. It's ACCEPTED here. I called to inquire about renting a space late afternoon Thursday, saw the space on Friday and was impressed by how friendly and knowledgeable both Diana and Allen were in answering all of my questions.  This is my first experience with renting a storage unit and I was unsure about the whole idea and process of doing this, but they quickly made me feel at ease and safe about moving some business/office stuff there temporarily.  I was impressed by how clean everything was...so clean I thought it was a new facility until they told me it had been there 10 years!  You can't even tell by looking at it. I highly recommend this location for your storage needs and for the excellent and friendly customer service provided by Diana and Allen.</Review>
